```
import websocket,ssl,_thread
import requests,time,random
from urllib import parse
from json import dumps, loads
import re

ws=websocket.create_connection("wss://hack.chat/chat-ws",sslopt={"cert_reqs": ssl.CERT_NONE})
ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"join","channel":"your-channel","nick":"dd","password":"h"}))
ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
def newserver(ws):
    while 1:
        try:
            time.sleep(120.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
            time.sleep(120.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
            time.sleep(60.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-gh"}))
            time.sleep(0.1)
            # ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-he"}))
            time.sleep(60.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
            time.sleep(120.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
            time.sleep(120.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-dd"}))
            time.sleep(0.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-gh"}))
            time.sleep(0.1)
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":"-悲伤的养鸡"}))
        except:
            ws=websocket.create_connection("wss://hack.chat/chat-ws",sslopt={"cert_reqs": ssl.CERT_NONE})
            ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"join","channel":"your-channel","nick":"jj","password":"h"}))
_thread.start_new_thread(newserver,(ws,))
while 1:
    newanswer=input('>')
    print("sending")
    ws.send(dumps({"cmd":"chat","text":newanswer }))

[/9Br2y] 4n0n4me
```python
from init import Handler
import threading,time

class ChickenRaiserHandler(Handler):
    def __init__(self, chatter, channel, nick, password, website_name=None):
        self.server_nick = 'ChiCkENmoYUVOs'
        self.owner = '4n0n4me'
        super().__init__(chatter, channel, nick, password, website_name)

    def wsendchat(self,text,nick=None):
        if not nick:
            nick = self.server_nick
        self.sendchat(f'/w {nick} {text}')

    def 繁殖小鸡(self):
        while True:
            self.wsendchat('-dd')
            self.wsendchat('已dd',self.owner)
            time.sleep(120.1)

    def 收获鸡蛋(self):
        while True:
            self.wsendchat('-gh')
            self.wsendchat('已gh',self.owner)
            time.sleep(300.1)

    def handle(self, ms_data):
            if ms_data['cmd'] == 'onlineSet':
                for nick in ms_data['nicks']:
                    if nick.lower() == 'ChiCkENmoYUVOs'.lower():
                        self.server_nick = nick
                        self.sendchat(f'已自动设定养鸡场服务器昵称为{self.server_nick}')
                threading.Thread(target=self.繁殖小鸡).start()
                threading.Thread(target=self.收获鸡蛋).start()
            if ms_data['cmd'] == 'chat':
                if ms_data['trip'] == '/9Br2y':
                    if len(ms_data['text'])>3:
                        if ms_data['text'][0:3] == '[] ':
                            self.server_nick = ms_data['text'][3:].strip('@ ')
                            self.sendchat(f'已将养鸡场服务器昵称设定为[{self.server_nick}]。')
                    else:
                        if ms_data['text'] == '[]':
                            self.owner = ms_data['nick']
                            self.sendchat(f'已将操作者昵称设定为[{self.owner}]')
```

[23:04:35]
[tssNfd] ccvv
Base64是网络上最常见的用于传输8Bit字节码的编码方式之一，Base64就是一种基于64个可打印字符来表示二进制数据的方法。可查看RFC2045～RFC2049，上面有MIME的详细规范。
Base64编码是从二进制到字符的过程，可用于在HTTP环境下传递较长的标识信息。采用Base64编码具有不可读性，需要解码后才能阅读。
Base64由于以上优点被广泛应用于计算机的各个领域，然而由于输出内容中包括两个以上“符号类”字符（+, /, =)，不同的应用场景又分别研制了Base64的各种“变种”。为统一和规范化Base64的输出，Base62x被视为无符号化的改进版本。

hash = (password) => {
    const sha = crypto.createHash('sha256');
    sha.update(password);
    return sha.digest('base64').substr(0, 6);
  };
